i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset[i]) {\n      return static_cast<uint64_t>(remaining - i);\n    }\n  }\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(remaining + 1);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Get the overflow bucket value for a given index.\n *\n * @param idx - bucket index\n * @return uint8_t - overflow value (4-bit)\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::GetOverflowBucketofIdx(uint16_t idx) const -> uint8_t {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n  size_t byte_idx = idx / 2;\n  if (byte_idx >= overflow_buckets_.size()) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n  if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n    return overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n  }\n  return (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds an element to the HyperLogLogPresto data structure.\n * @param val - value to add\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = HashUtil::Hash(val);\n  std::bitset<64> bits = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract top n_leading_bits_ bits as bucket index\n  uint64_t idx = 0;\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_leading_bits_; i++) {\n    idx = (idx << 1) | (bits[63 - i] ? 1 : 0);\n  }\n\n  // Compute position of leftmost one in remaining bits\n  uint64_t pos = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bits);\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Get current bucket value\n  size_t byte_idx = idx / 2;\n  uint8_t current_dense;\n  uint8_t current_overflow;\n\n  if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n    current_dense = dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n    current_overflow = overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n  } else {\n    current_dense = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n    current_overflow = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n  }\n\n  // Combined current value: overflow * 16 + dense? No, let's think...\n  // The value is split: lower 4 bits in dense, upper 4 bits in overflow\n  // total value = (overflow << 4) | dense\n  // But that would be 8-bit total, supporting values 0-255\n  // Actually, let's use: value = overflow_val * 16 + dense_val\n  // where overflow_val and dense_val are each 4-bit (0-15)\n  // This gives max value of 15*16 + 15 = 255\n\n  // For HLL with b=4, max position = 64-4+1 = 61, which fits in 6 bits\n  // So 4+4=8 bits is more than enough\n\n  uint64_t current_val = (static_cast<uint64_t>(current_overflow) << 4) | current_dense;\n\n  if (pos > current_val) {\n    uint8_t new_dense = static_cast<uint8_t>(pos & 0x0F);\n    uint8_t new_overflow = static_cast<uint8_t>((pos >> 4) & 0x0F);\n\n    if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n      dense_bucket_[byte_idx] = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0xF0) | new_dense;\n      overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0xF0) | new_overflow;\n    } else {\n      dense_bucket_[byte_idx] = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F) | (new_dense << 4);\n      overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F) | (new_overflow << 4);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Estimates the cardinality of the data seen so far.\n * @return size_t - estimated cardinality\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::EstimateCardinality() const -> size_t {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n\n  size_t m = 1ULL << n_leading_bits_;\n  double sum = 0.0;\n\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < m; i++) {\n    size_t byte_idx = i / 2;\n    uint8_t dense_val;\n    uint8_t overflow_val;\n\n    if (i % 2 == 0) {\n      dense_val = dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n      overflow_val = overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n    } else {\n      dense_val = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n      overflow_val = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n    }\n\n    uint64_t reg_val = (static_cast<uint64_t>(overflow_val) << 4) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n  return static_cast<size_t>(std::floor(estimate));\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1207,"cache_read_input_tokens":26709,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1207,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e7a7d4ec-b533-41a4-9be8-22b40a320e77","uuid":"d3af6463-f8cf-4a96-b69c-0f0b4c97544c"}

i < n_leading_bits_; i++) {\n    idx = (idx << 1) | (bits[63 - i] ? 1 : 0);\n  }\n\n  // Compute position of leftmost one in remaining bits\n  uint64_t pos = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bits);\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Get current bucket value\n  size_t byte_idx = idx / 2;\n  uint8_t current_dense;\n  uint8_t current_overflow;\n\n  if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n    current_dense = dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n    current_overflow = overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n  } else {\n    current_dense = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n    current_overflow = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n  }\n\n  // Combined current value: overflow * 16 + dense? No, let's think...\n  // The value is split: lower 4 bits in dense, upper 4 bits in overflow\n  // total value = (overflow << 4) | dense\n  // But that would be 8-bit total, supporting values 0-255\n  // Actually, let's use: value = overflow_val * 16 + dense_val\n  // where overflow_val and dense_val are each 4-bit (0-15)\n  // This gives max value of 15*16 + 15 = 255\n\n  // For HLL with b=4, max position = 64-4+1 = 61, which fits in 6 bits\n  // So 4+4=8 bits is more than enough\n\n  uint64_t current_val = (static_cast<uint64_t>(current_overflow) << 4) | current_dense;\n\n  if (pos > current_val) {\n    uint8_t new_dense = static_cast<uint8_t>(pos & 0x0F);\n    uint8_t new_overflow = static_cast<uint8_t>((pos >> 4) & 0x0F);\n\n    if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n      dense_bucket_[byte_idx] = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0xF0) | new_dense;\n      overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0xF0) | new_overflow;\n    } else {\n      dense_bucket_[byte_idx] = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F) | (new_dense << 4);\n      overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F) | (new_overflow << 4);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Estimates the cardinality of the data seen so far.\n * @return size_t - estimated cardinality\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::EstimateCardinality() const -> size_t {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n\n  size_t m = 1ULL << n_leading_bits_;\n  double sum = 0.0;\n\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < m; i++) {\n    size_t byte_idx = i / 2;\n    uint8_t dense_val;\n    uint8_t overflow_val;\n\n    if (i % 2 == 0) {\n      dense_val = dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n      overflow_val = overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n    } else {\n      dense_val = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n      overflow_val = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n    }\n\n    uint64_t reg_val = (static_cast<uint64_t>(overflow_val) << 4) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n  return static_cast<size_t>(std::floor(estimate));\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01G2bC3Dm8WAeNAFXCCXaGsE","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Wait, if both hyperloglog.h and hyperloglog_presto.h define `const double CONSTANT = 0.79402;`, and they're both included in the same translation unit, there will be a duplicate definition error. Let me use a different approach - use `static const double` or define it only once.\n\nActually, `const` at namespace scope in C++ has internal linkage, so defining `const double CONSTANT = 0.79402;` in a header included in multiple translation units is fine - each TU gets its own copy with internal linkage.\n\nBut if both headers are included in the same TU (like when hyperloglog_test.cpp includes both), there will be a redefinition error.\n\n\nI could move the constant to a shared location, use `inline constexpr` to allow multiple definitions, or just put it in the cpp files instead of the headers. I think moving it to the implementation files is the cleanest binary representation of hash\n * @return uint64_t - position of leftmost one (1-indexed from MSB of\n *                    remaining bits)\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<64> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // We check bits from position (63 - n_bits_) down to 0\n  // (since bitset bit 63 is MSB, bit 0 is LSB)\n  // The \"remaining\" bits are bits [63 - n_bits_] down to [0]\n  int remaining = 64 - n_bits_;\n  for (int i = remaining - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset[i]) {\n      // Position from left in the remaining bits\n      return static_cast<uint64_t>(remaining - i);\n    }\n  }\n  // All remaining bits are 0\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(remaining + 1);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds an element to the HyperLogLog data structure.\n * @param val - value to add\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = HashUtil::Hash(val);\n  std::bitset<64> bits = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract top n_bits_ bits as register index\n  // bits[63] is the MSB\n  uint64_t idx = 0;\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_bits_; i++) {\n    idx = (idx << 1) | (bits[63 - i] ? 1 : 0);\n  }\n\n  // Compute position of leftmost one in remaining bits\n  uint64_t pos = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bits);\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n  if (pos > registers_[idx]) {\n    registers_[idx] = static_cast<uint8_t>(pos);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Estimates the cardinality of the data seen so far.\n * @return size_t - estimated cardinality\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::EstimateCardinality() const -> size_t {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n\n  size_t m = registers_.size();\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < m; i++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n  return static_cast<size_t>(std::floor(estimate));\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":14,"oldLines":6,"newStart":14,"newLines":8,"lines":[" "," namespace bustub {"," ","+static constexpr double CONSTANT = 0.79402;","+"," /** @brief Parameterized constructor. */"," template <typename KeyType>"," HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : n_bits_(n_bits) {"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

static_cast<uint64_t>(remaining + 1);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Get the overflow bucket value for a given index.\n *\n * @param idx - bucket index\n * @return uint8_t - overflow value (4-bit)\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::GetOverflowBucketofIdx(uint16_t idx) const -> uint8_t {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n  size_t byte_idx = idx / 2;\n  if (byte_idx >= overflow_buckets_.size()) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n  if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n    return overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n  }\n  return (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds an element to the HyperLogLogPresto data structure.\n * @param val - value to add\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = HashUtil::Hash(val);\n  std::bitset<64> bits = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract top n_leading_bits_ bits as bucket index\n  uint64_t idx = 0;\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_leading_bits_; i++) {\n    idx = (idx << 1) | (bits[63 - i] ? 1 : 0);\n  }\n\n  // Compute position of leftmost one in remaining bits\n  uint64_t pos = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bits);\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Get current bucket value\n  size_t byte_idx = idx / 2;\n  uint8_t current_dense;\n  uint8_t current_overflow;\n\n  if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n    current_dense = dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n    current_overflow = overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n  } else {\n    current_dense = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n    current_overflow = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n  }\n\n  // Combined current value: overflow * 16 + dense? No, let's think...\n  // The value is split: lower 4 bits in dense, upper 4 bits in overflow\n  // total value = (overflow << 4) | dense\n  // But that would be 8-bit total, supporting values 0-255\n  // Actually, let's use: value = overflow_val * 16 + dense_val\n  // where overflow_val and dense_val are each 4-bit (0-15)\n  // This gives max value of 15*16 + 15 = 255\n\n  // For HLL with b=4, max position = 64-4+1 = 61, which fits in 6 bits\n  // So 4+4=8 bits is more than enough\n\n  uint64_t current_val = (static_cast<uint64_t>(current_overflow) << 4) | current_dense;\n\n  if (pos > current_val) {\n    uint8_t new_dense = static_cast<uint8_t>(pos & 0x0F);\n    uint8_t new_overflow = static_cast<uint8_t>((pos >> 4) & 0x0F);\n\n    if (idx % 2 == 0) {\n      dense_bucket_[byte_idx] = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0xF0) | new_dense;\n      overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0xF0) | new_overflow;\n    } else {\n      dense_bucket_[byte_idx] = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F) | (new_dense << 4);\n      overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F) | (new_overflow << 4);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Estimates the cardinality of the data seen so far.\n * @return size_t - estimated cardinality\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::EstimateCardinality() const -> size_t {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n\n  size_t m = 1ULL << n_leading_bits_;\n  double sum = 0.0;\n\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < m; i++) {\n    size_t byte_idx = i / 2;\n    uint8_t dense_val;\n    uint8_t overflow_val;\n\n    if (i % 2 == 0) {\n      dense_val = dense_bucket_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n      overflow_val = overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] & 0x0F;\n    } else {\n      dense_val = (dense_bucket_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n      overflow_val = (overflow_buckets_[byte_idx] >> 4) & 0x0F;\n    }\n\n    uint64_t reg_val = (static_cast<uint64_t>(overflow_val) << 4) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(reg_val));\n  }\n\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n  return static_cast<size_t>(std::floor(estimate));\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":14,"oldLines":6,"newStart":14,"newLines":8,"lines":[" "," namespace bustub {"," ","+static constexpr double CONSTANT = 0.79402;","+"," /** @brief Parameterized constructor. */"," template <typename KeyType>"," HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits) : n_leading_bits_(n_leading_bits) {"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

n_bits_) down to 0\n  // (since bitset bit 63 is MSB, bit 0 is LSB)\n  // The \"remaining\" bits are bits [63 - n_bits_] down to [0]\n  int remaining = 64 - n_bits_;\n  for (int i = remaining - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset[i]) {\n      // Position from left in the remaining bits\n      return static_cast<uint64_t>(remaining - The test.cpp includes hyperloglog.h and hyperloglog_presto.h. With header guards, each header is included only once).\n\n\nActually, let me trace through this more carefully. The test includes hyperloglog.h directly, which defines CONSTANT in that translation unit. When it includes hyperloglog_presto.h, that header doesn't pull in hyperloglog.h anymore, so CONSTANT isn't redefined.
